 twitter
 com / zgd9s1szj4— ANI (@ani)january 21, 2018 Efforts to bring Syrian chemical weapons under international control began in Geneva on Thursday where top leaders of the US and Russia negotiated Moscow's four-phase plan to avert any military intervention
 vahiin, rus ke raashtrapati vladimir putin ne taaja sankat par americanyon se nijee taur par apil kii
 Negotiations on a four-phase plan between US Secretary of State John Kerry and Russian Foreign Minister Sergei Lavrov in Geneva will take place tomorrow and may continue until Saturday
 rus kii yojana main syria kaa rasinic hathiyaar rokthaam sanghathan main shaamil hona bhi shaamil he
 The plan is to draft in this dialogue when and how Syria will hand over the stockpiles of chemical weapons
 is vaarta se purv raashtrapati bashar al asad ne aaj kaha ki syria rus ke prastaav ke kaaran apane rasinic hathiyaaron kaa aatmasamarpan karne par sahamat hua he, america dhamkee ke kaaran nahin
 Assad told Russia's official channel Russia 24 that Syria was handing over its chemical weapons under international control due to Russia, the US threat would have no effect on the decision to hand over chemical weapons
 masco dwaara is saptaah kii shuruuaat main pesh kii gai yojana kaa uddeshy syrian raashtrapati bashar al asad ke shashan ke khilaaf america nit sainya hamale ko rokna he
 The United States holds Assad responsible for the killing of nearly 1000 civilians with chemical weapons outside Damascus on 21 August
 rus ke kommarcent daily akhbaar ne aaj pehali baar syrian prashasan ke rasinic hathiyaaron kii supurdagee ke liye america ko rus dwaara di gai chaar charniya yojana kii jaankaree saarvajanik kii
 On the other hand, raising voice against the US military offensive against the Assad regime, Putin has written an article in the 'new York Times' in which he has spoken directly to the American public and their leaders on the Syrian issue
 putin ne lekh ‘e pli for kaashan fram rashia’ ke jariye chetaya he ki agar prabhavishali desh suraksha parishad kii manjuuri ke bagaiyr sainya karrwai karte hai to sanyukt raashtra kaa hashr bhi ‘lig for neshns’ jaisaa ho jayega
 He wrote, "despite strong opposition from various countries, major political parties, and various religious leaders, including the pope, America's attack on Syria will prey on large numbers of innocent people, escalate conflict and spread beyond the Syrian borders
" ’’ Putin reiterated Russia's view that the August 21 attack was probably intended to provoke the intervention of its powerful patrons by opposition forces
 kommarcent ne ek roosi kootnithik sutara ke hawaale se kaha ki pehle charan main damishq rasinic hathiyaar nishedh sanghathan kaa sadsy banegaa
 After this, Syria will have to declare an arsenal of chemical weapons and their manufacturing site
 tisare charan ke tahat opisidblyoo ke nirikshakon ko syria main aakar jaanch karne kii anumati milegi
 The final phase will be quite decisive, in which it will be decided with the cooperation of inspectors how to destroy these weapons
 is bich, syria ke vidrohi sanghathan ‘free sirian army’ ne rus kii yojana ko khaarij kar diya or kaha ki yah yojana bahut aage nahin badhegi
 General Salim Idris of this organization said that we request that the main conspirator of the crime be produced before the International Criminal Court while keeping the chemical weapons under international control
 tippaniyan US President Barack Obama yesterday postponed a military strike against Syria but said that the attack would be carried out if Russia's plan failed
 obama ko syria par hamale ke prastaav ko lekar america congress or america janata se virodh kaa saamana karnaa pad rahaa he
 At the same time, Russian President Vladimir Putin personally appealed to the Americans on the latest crisis
 geneva main america videsh mantri jon kerri or rus ke videsh mantri sarajei lavarove ke bich chaar charnon kii yojana par vaarta kal bhi hogi or yah shanivaar tak jari rah sakati he
 Russia's plan also includes Syria's involvement in the Chemical Weapons Prevention Organization
 is vaarta main yojana kaa masauda taiyaar hona he ki syria kab or kaise rasinic hathiyaaron ke jakhiron ko saunpega
 Prior to the talks, President Bashar al-assad said today that Syria has agreed to surrender its chemical weapons because of Russia's proposal, not because of US intimidation
 asad ne rus ke sarkari channel ‘rashia 24’ se kaha ki syria rus ke kaaran apane rasinic hathiyaaron ko antarrashtriya niyantran main saunp rahaa he, america dhamkee kaa rasinic hathiyaar saunpane ke faisle par koi prabhaav nahin padegaa
 The plan, introduced earlier this week by Moscow, aims to prevent a us-led military offensive against Syrian President Bashar al-assad's regime
 america asad ko 21 agast ko damishq ke baahar rasinic hathiyaar se kareeb 1000 nagarikon kii hatya ke liye jimmedaar maanata he
 Russia's Kommersant Daily newspaper today revealed for the first time the information about the four-phase plan given by Russia to the US for the delivery of chemical weapons of the Syrian administration
 udhar, asad shashan ke khilaaf america sainya hamale ke khilaaf aawaaj uthaate hue putin ne ‘neuyark times’ main ek lekh likhaa he jisamen unhone syria ke mudde par ‘sidhe america janata or unke netaaon’ se baat kii he
 Putin has warned through the article 'A Plea for Kashan from Russia' that if the influential countries take military action without the approval of the Security Council, then the UN will also face the fate of the League for Nations
 unhone likhaa, ‘‘kai deshon, pramukh raajnneetik dalon or pope samet vibhinn dharmik netaaon ke kade virodh ke baavjood syria par america ke hamale se badi sankhya main nirdosh log shikaar honge, sangharsh badhegaa or yah syrian simaaon ke baahar tak fail jayega
 '' putin ne rus ke is nazariye ko doharaaya ki 21 agast kaa hamalaa sambhavat: vipakshi balon dwaara apane shaktishaalee sangrakshakon ke hastkshep ko uksaane ke liye kiya gaya
 Kommersant quoted a Russian diplomatic source as saying that Damascus would become a member of the Chemical Weapons Prohibition Organization in the first phase
 iske baad syria ko rasinic hathiyaaron ke shastraagaar or unke nirmaan sthal kii ghoshnaa kerani hogi
 As part of the third phase, OPCW inspectors will be allowed to come to Syria to conduct investigations
 antim charan kaaphi nirnaayak hoga, jisamen nirikshakon ke sahyog se yah tay kiya jayega ki in hathiyaaron ko nasht kaise kiya jaae
 Meanwhile, the Syrian rebel organization 'free Syrian Army' rejected Russia's plan and said the plan would not go ahead much
 is sanghathan ke general saleem idris ne kaha ki ham anurodh karte hai ki rasinic hathiyaaron ko antarrashtriya niyantran main rakhane ke saath aparaadh ke mukhya sajeeshkarta ko antarrashtriya aparaadh adaalat ke saamne pesh kiya jaae
